    42	func NewPrometheusCRWatcher(
    43	        ctx context.Context,
    44	        logger logr.Logger,
    45	        client kubernetes.Interface,
    46	        monitoringclient monitoringclient.Interface,
    47	        cfg allocatorconfig.Config,
    48	) (*PrometheusCRWatcher, error) {
    49	        promLogger := slog.New(slog.NewTextHandler(os.Stderr, &slog.HandlerOptions{Level: slog.LevelWarn}))
    50	        slogger := slog.New(logr.ToSlogHandler(logger))
    51	        var resourceSelector *prometheus.ResourceSelector
    52	
    53	        allowList, denyList := cfg.PrometheusCR.GetAllowDenyLists()
    54	
    55	        factory := informers.NewMonitoringInformerFactories(allowList, denyList, monitoringclient, allocatorconfig.DefaultResyncTime, nil)
    56	
    57	        monitoringInformers, err := getInformers(cfg, factory, monitoringclient)
    58	        if err != nil {
    59	                return nil, err
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        // we want to use endpointslices by default
    63	        serviceDiscoveryRole := monitoringv1.ServiceDiscoveryRole("EndpointSlice")
    64	
    65	        // TODO: We should make these durations configurable
    66	        prom := &monitoringv1.Prometheus{
    67	                ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
    68	                        Namespace: cfg.CollectorNamespace,
    69	                },
    70	                Spec: monitoringv1.PrometheusSpec{
    71	                        CommonPrometheusFields: monitoringv1.CommonPrometheusFields{
    72	                                ScrapeInterval:                  monitoringv1.Duration(cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeInterval.String()),
    73	                                PodMonitorSelector:              cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorSelector,
    74	                                PodMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
    75	                                ServiceMonitorSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorSelector,
    76	                                ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector: cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
    77	                                ScrapeConfigSelector:            cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigSelector,
    78	                                ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
    79	                                ProbeSelector:                   cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeSelector,
    80	                                ProbeNamespaceSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeNamespaceSelector,
    81	                                ServiceDiscoveryRole:            &serviceDiscoveryRole,
    82	                                Version:                         "2.55.1", // fix Prometheus version 2 to avoid generating incompatible config
    83	                                ScrapeProtocols:                 cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeProtocols,
    84	                        },
    85	                        EvaluationInterval: monitoringv1.Duration("30s"),
    86	                },
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        generator, err := prometheus.NewConfigGenerator(promLogger, prom, prometheus.WithEndpointSliceSupport(), prometheus.WithInlineTLSConfig())
    90	
    91	        if err != nil {
    92	                return nil, err
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        store := assets.NewStoreBuilder(client.CoreV1(), client.CoreV1())
    96	        promRegisterer := prometheusgoclient.NewRegistry()
    97	        operatorMetrics := operator.NewMetrics(promRegisterer)
    98	        eventRecorderFactory := operator.NewEventRecorderFactory(false)
    99	        eventRecorder := eventRecorderFactory(client, "target-allocator")
   100	
   101	        var nsMonInf cache.SharedIndexInformer
   102	        getNamespaceInformerErr := retry.OnError(retry.DefaultRetry,
   103	                func(err error) bool {
   104	                        logger.Error(err, "Retrying namespace informer creation in promOperator CRD watcher")
   105	                        return true
   106	                }, func() error {
   107	                        nsMonInf, err = getNamespaceInformer(ctx, allowList, denyList, promLogger, client, operatorMetrics)
   108	                        return err
   109	                })
   110	        if getNamespaceInformerErr != nil {
   111	                logger.Error(getNamespaceInformerErr, "Failed to create namespace informer in promOperator CRD watcher")
   112	                return nil, getNamespaceInformerErr
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        resourceSelector, err = prometheus.NewResourceSelector(slogger, prom, store, nsMonInf, operatorMetrics, eventRecorder)
   116	        if err != nil {
   117	                logger.Error(err, "Failed to create resource selector in promOperator CRD watcher")
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        return &PrometheusCRWatcher{
   121	                logger:                          slogger,
   122	                kubeMonitoringClient:            monitoringclient,
   123	                k8sClient:                       client,
   124	                informers:                       monitoringInformers,
   125	                nsInformer:                      nsMonInf,
   126	                stopChannel:                     make(chan struct{}),
   127	                eventInterval:                   minEventInterval,
   128	                configGenerator:                 generator,
   129	                kubeConfigPath:                  cfg.KubeConfigFilePath,
   130	                podMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   131	                serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector: cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   132	                scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
   133	                probeNamespaceSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeNamespaceSelector,
   134	                resourceSelector:                resourceSelector,
   135	                store:                           store,
   136	                prometheusCR:                    prom,
   137	        }, nil
   138	}

   159	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) Informers() map[string]*informers.ForResource {
   160	return w.informers
   161	}
   162	
   163	func getNamespaceInformer(ctx context.Context, allowList, denyList map[string]struct{}, promOperatorLogger *slog.Logger, clientset kubernetes.Interface, operatorMetrics *operator.Metrics) (cache.SharedIndexInformer, error) {
   164	        kubernetesVersion, err := clientset.Discovery().ServerVersion()
   165	        if err != nil {
   166	                return nil, err
   167	        }
   168	        kubernetesSemverVersion, err := semver.ParseTolerant(kubernetesVersion.String())
   169	        if err != nil {
   170	                return nil, err
   171	        }
   172	        lw, _, err := listwatch.NewNamespaceListWatchFromClient(
   173	                ctx,
   174	                promOperatorLogger,
   175	                kubernetesSemverVersion,
   176	                clientset.CoreV1(),
   177	                clientset.AuthorizationV1().SelfSubjectAccessReviews(),
   178	                allowList,
   179	                denyList,
   180	        )
   181	        if err != nil {
   182	                return nil, err
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        return cache.NewSharedIndexInformer(
   186	                operatorMetrics.NewInstrumentedListerWatcher(lw),
   187	                &v1.Namespace{}, resyncPeriod, cache.Indexers{},
   188	        ), nil
   189	
   190	}
   191	
   192	func getInformers(
   193	cfg allocatorconfig.Config,
   194	factory informers.FactoriesForNamespaces,
   195	monitoringclient monitoringclient.Interface,
   196	) (map[string]*informers.ForResource, error) {
   197	informersMap := make(map[string]*informers.ForResource)
   198	
   199	gv := monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion
   200	agv := promv1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion
   201	
   202	resources := []struct {
   203	name     string
   204	selector *metav1.LabelSelector
   205	resource string
   206	gv       metav1.GroupVersion
   207	}{
   208	{monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorSelector, monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName, gv},
   209	{monitoringv1.PodMonitorName, cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorSelector, monitoringv1.PodMonitorName, gv},
   210	{monitoringv1.ProbeName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeSelector, monitoringv1.ProbeName, gv},
   211	{promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigSelector, promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName, agv},
   212	}
   213	
   214	for _, res := range resources {
   215	if res.selector == nil {
   216	continue
   217	}
   218	
   219	// Check if CRD exists
   220	if _, err := monitoringclient.Discovery().ServerResourcesForGroupVersion(res.gv.String()); err != nil {
   221	// This is a bit rough check, but let's refine it.
   222	// Actually, the client-go discovery can be used.
   223	}
   224	
   225	inf, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, res.gv.WithResource(res.resource))
   226	if err != nil {
   227	return nil, err
   228	}
   229	informersMap[res.name] = inf
   230	}
   231	
   232	return informersMap, nil
   233	}
   234	
   235	// Watch wrapped informers and wait for an initial sync.
   236	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) Watch(upstreamEvents chan Event, upstreamErrors chan error) error {
   237	        success := true
   238	        // this channel needs to be buffered because notifications are asynchronous and neither producers nor consumers wait
   239	        notifyEvents := make(chan struct{}, 1)
   240	
   241	        if w.nsInformer != nil {
   242	                go w.nsInformer.Run(w.stopChannel)
   243	                if ok := w.WaitForNamedCacheSync("namespace", w.nsInformer.HasSynced); !ok {
   244	                        success = false
   245	                }
   246	
   247	                _, _ = w.nsInformer.AddEventHandler(cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   248	                        UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
   249	                                old := oldObj.(*v1.Namespace)
   250	                                cur := newObj.(*v1.Namespace)
   251	
   252	                                // Periodic resync may resend the Namespace without changes
   253	                                // in-between.
   254	                                if old.ResourceVersion == cur.ResourceVersion {
   255	                                        return
   256	                                }
   257	
   258	                                for name, selector := range map[string]*metav1.LabelSelector{
   259	                                        "PodMonitorNamespaceSelector":     w.podMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   260	                                        "ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector": w.serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
   261	                                        "ProbeNamespaceSelector":          w.probeNamespaceSelector,
   262	                                        "ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector":   w.scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
   263	                                } {
   264	                                        sync, err := k8sutil.LabelSelectionHasChanged(old.Labels, cur.Labels, selector)
   265	                                        if err != nil {
   266	                                                w.logger.Error("Failed to check label selection between namespaces while handling namespace updates", "selector", name, "error", err)
   267	                                                return
   268	                                        }
   269	
   270	                                        if sync {
   271	                                                select {
   272	                                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   273	                                                default:
   274	                                                }
   275	                                                return
   276	                                        }
   277	                                }
   278	                        },
   279	                })
   280	        } else {
   281	                w.logger.Info("Unable to watch namespaces since namespace informer is nil")
   282	        }
   283	
   284	        for name, resource := range w.informers {
   285	                resource.Start(w.stopChannel)
   286	
   287	                if ok := w.WaitForNamedCacheSync(name, resource.HasSynced); !ok {
   288	                        w.logger.Info("skipping informer", "informer", name)
   289	                        continue
   290	                }
   291	
   292	                // only send an event notification if there isn't one already
   293	                resource.AddEventHandler(cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
   294	                        // these functions only write to the notification channel if it's empty to avoid blocking
   295	                        // if scrape config updates are being rate-limited
   296	                        AddFunc: func(obj interface{}) {
   297	                                select {
   298	                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   299	                                default:
   300	                                }
   301	                        },
   302	                        UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
   303	                                select {
   304	                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   305	                                default:
   306	                                }
   307	                        },
   308	                        DeleteFunc: func(obj interface{}) {
   309	                                select {
   310	                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
   311	                                default:
   312	                                }
   313	                        },
   314	                })
   315	        }
   316	        if !success {
   317	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to sync one of the caches")
   318	        }
   319	
   320	        // limit the rate of outgoing events
   321	        w.rateLimitedEventSender(upstreamEvents, notifyEvents)
   322	
   323	        <-w.stopChannel
   324	        return nil
   325	}
   326	
   327	// rateLimitedEventSender sends events to the upstreamEvents channel whenever it gets a notification on the notifyEvents channel,
   328	// but not more frequently than once per w.eventPeriod.
   329	func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) rateLimitedEventSender(upstreamEvents chan Event, notifyEvents chan struct{}) {
   330	        ticker := time.NewTicker(w.eventInterval)
   331	        defer ticker.Stop()
   332	
   333	        event := Event{
   334	                Source:  EventSourcePrometheusCR,
   335	                Watcher: Watcher(w),
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        for {
   339	                select {
   340	                case <-w.stopChannel:
   341	                        return
   342	                case <-ticker.C: // throttle events to avoid excessive updates
   343	                        select {
   344	             <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

' --new_str 'func getInformers(
	slogger *slog.Logger,
	cfg allocatorconfig.Config,
	factory informers.FactoriesForNamespaces,
	monitoringclient monitoringclient.Interface,
) (map[string]*informers.ForResource, error) {
	informersMap := make(map[string]*informers.ForResource)

	gv := monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion
	agv := promv1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion

	resources := []struct {
		name     string
		selector *metav1.LabelSelector
		resource string
		gv       metav1.GroupVersion
	}{
		{monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorSelector, monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName, gv},
		{monitoringv1.PodMonitorName, cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorSelector, monitoringv1.PodMonitorName, gv},
		{monitoringv1.ProbeName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeSelector, monitoringv1.ProbeName, gv},
		{promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigSelector, promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName, agv},
	}

	for _, res := range resources {
		if res.selector == nil {
			continue
		}

		// Check if CRD exists
		apiResources, err := monitoringclient.Discovery().ServerResourcesForGroupVersion(res.gv.String())
		if err != nil {
			slogger.Warn("CRD not found, skipping informer", "groupVersion", res.gv.String(), "resource", res.resource)
			continue
		}
		found := false
		for _, resource := range apiResources.APIResources {
			if resource.Name == res.resource {
				found = true
				break
			}
		}
		if !found {
			slogger.Warn("CRD found but resource not found, skipping informer", "groupVersion", res.gv.String(), "resource", res.resource)
			continue
		}

		inf, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, res.gv.WithResource(res.resource))
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
		informersMap[res.name] = inf
	}

	return informersMap, nil
}

/usr/bin/python3 -c '
import os
content = open("/testbed/cmd/otel-allocator/internal/watcher/promOperator.go").read()

new_get_informers = """func getInformers(
	slogger *slog.Logger,
	cfg allocatorconfig.Config,
	factory informers.FactoriesForNamespaces,
	monitoringclient monitoringclient.Interface,
) (map[string]*informers.ForResource, error) {
	informersMap := make(map[string]*informers.ForResource)

	gv := monitoringv1.SchemeGroupVersion
	agv := promv1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion

	resources := []struct {
		name     string
		selector *metav1.LabelSelector
		resource string
		gv       metav1.GroupVersion
	}{
		{monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorSelector, monitoringv1.ServiceMonitorName, gv},
		{monitoringv1.PodMonitorName, cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorSelector, monitoringv1.PodMonitorName, gv},
		{monitoringv1.ProbeName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeSelector, monitoringv1.ProbeName, gv},
		{promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName, cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigSelector, promv1alpha1.ScrapeConfigName, agv},
	}

	for _, res := range resources {
		if res.selector == nil {
			continue
		}

		// Check if CRD exists
		apiResources, err := monitoringclient.Discovery().ServerResourcesForGroupVersion(res.gv.String())
		if err != nil {
			slogger.Warn("CRD not found, skipping informer", "groupVersion", res.gv.String(), "resource", res.resource)
			continue
		}
		found := false
		for _, resource := range apiResources.APIResources {
			if resource.Name == res.resource {
				found = true
				break
			}
		}
		if !found {
			slogger.Warn("CRD found but resource not found, skipping informer", "groupVersion", res.gv.String(), "resource", res.resource)
			continue
		}

		inf, err := informers.NewInformersForResource(factory, res.gv.WithResource(res.resource))
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
		informersMap[res.name] = inf
	}

	return informersMap, nil
}"""

import re
content = re.sub(r"func getInformers\(.*?\) \(map\[string\]\*informers\.ForResource, error\) \{.*?^}", new_get_informers, content, flags=re.DOTALL | re.MULTILINE)
content = content.replace("monitoringInformers, err := getInformers(cfg, factory, monitoringclient)", "monitoringInformers, err := getInformers(slogger, cfg, factory, monitoringclient)")

with open("/testbed/cmd/otel-allocator/internal/watcher/promOperator.go", "w") as f:
    f.write(content)

This prevents errors when some CRDs like `Probe` or `ScrapeConfig` are not installed in the cluster.\n\n### Changes Made:\n1.  **Modified `getInformers` in `cmd/otel-allocator/internal/watcher/promOperator.go`**:\n    *   The function now accepts a logger and the allocator configuration.\n    *   It iterates through the expected CRDs (`ServiceMonitor`, `PodMonitor`, `Probe`, and `ScrapeConfig`).\n    *   For each resource, it first checks if it's enabled in the configuration via its respective selector.\n    *   If enabled, it uses the Kubernetes Discovery API to verify if the corresponding CRD is actually present in the cluster.\n    *   If a CRD or its resource is missing, it logs a warning and skips the creation of that specific informer, rather than allowing the allocator to fail later when starting the informer.\n\n2.  **Updated `NewPrometheusCRWatcher`**:\n    *   Modified the call to `getInformers` to pass the required logger and +                                PodMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
+                                ServiceMonitorSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorSelector,

+
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        store := assets.NewStoreBuilder(client.CoreV1(), client.CoreV1())
+        promRegisterer := prometheusgoclient.NewRegistry()
+        operatorMetrics := operator.NewMetrics(promRegisterer)
+        eventRecorderFactory := operator.NewEventRecorderFactory(false)
+        eventRecorder := eventRecorderFactory(client, "target-allocator")
+
+        var nsMonInf cache.SharedIndexInformer
+        getNamespaceInformerErr := retry.OnError(retry.DefaultRetry,
+                func(err error) bool {
+                        logger.Error(err, "Retrying namespace informer creation in promOperator CRD watcher")
+                        return true
+                }, func() error {
+                        nsMonInf, err = getNamespaceInformer(ctx, allowList, denyList, promLogger, client, operatorMetrics)
+                        return err
+                })
+        if getNamespaceInformerErr != nil {
+                logger.Error(getNamespaceInformerErr, "Failed to create namespace informer in promOperator CRD watcher")
+                return nil, getNamespaceInformerErr
+        }
+
+        resourceSelector, err = prometheus.NewResourceSelector(slogger, prom, store, nsMonInf, operatorMetrics, eventRecorder)
+        if err != nil {
+                logger.Error(err, "Failed to create resource selector in promOperator CRD watcher")
+        }
+
+        return &PrometheusCRWatcher{
+                logger:                          slogger,
+                kubeMonitoringClient:            monitoringclient,
+                k8sClient:                       client,
+                informers:                       monitoringInformers,
+                nsInformer:                      nsMonInf,
+                stopChannel:                     make(chan struct{}),
+                eventInterval:                   minEventInterval,
+                configGenerator:                 generator,
+                kubeConfigPath:                  cfg.KubeConfigFilePath,
+                podMonitorNamespaceSelector:     cfg.PrometheusCR.PodMonitorNamespaceSelector,
+                serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector: cfg.PrometheusCR.ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
+                scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector:   cfg.PrometheusCR.ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
+                probeNamespaceSelector:          cfg.PrometheusCR.ProbeNamespaceSelector,
+                resourceSelector:                resourceSelector,
+                store:                           store,
+                prometheusCR:                    prom,
+        }, nil
 }

-	scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector   *metav1.LabelSelector
-	probeNamespaceSelector          *metav1.LabelSelector

-	store                           *assets.StoreBuilder
-	prometheusCR                    *monitoringv1.Prometheus
+        logger                          *slog.Logger
+        kubeMonitoringClient            monitoringclient.Interface
+        k8sClient                       kubernetes.Interface
+        informers                       map[string]*informers.ForResource
+        nsInformer                      cache.SharedIndexInformer

+        stopChannel                     chan struct{}
+        configGenerator                 *prometheus.ConfigGenerator
+        kubeConfigPath                  string

+        serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector *metav1.LabelSelector
+        scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector   *metav1.LabelSelector
+        probeNamespaceSelector          *metav1.LabelSelector
+        resourceSelector                *prometheus.ResourceSelector
+        store                           *assets.StoreBuilder

+        success := true
+        // this channel needs to be buffered because notifications are asynchronous and neither producers nor consumers wait
+        notifyEvents := make(chan struct{}, 1)

+        if w.nsInformer != nil {
+                go w.nsInformer.Run(w.stopChannel)
+                if ok := w.WaitForNamedCacheSync("namespace", w.nsInformer.HasSynced); !ok {
+                        success = false
+                }
+
+                _, _ = w.nsInformer.AddEventHandler(cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
+                        UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
+                                old := oldObj.(*v1.Namespace)
+                                cur := newObj.(*v1.Namespace)
+
+                                // Periodic resync may resend the Namespace without changes
+                                // in-between.
+                                if old.ResourceVersion == cur.ResourceVersion {
+                                        return
+                                }
+
+                                for name, selector := range map[string]*metav1.LabelSelector{
+                                        "PodMonitorNamespaceSelector":     w.podMonitorNamespaceSelector,
+                                        "ServiceMonitorNamespaceSelector": w.serviceMonitorNamespaceSelector,
+                                        "ProbeNamespaceSelector":          w.probeNamespaceSelector,
+                                        "ScrapeConfigNamespaceSelector":   w.scrapeConfigNamespaceSelector,
+                                } {
+                                        sync, err := k8sutil.LabelSelectionHasChanged(old.Labels, cur.Labels, selector)
+                                        if err != nil {
+                                                w.logger.Error("Failed to check label selection between namespaces while handling namespace updates", "selector", name, "error", err)
+                                                return
+                                        }
+

+                                                select {
+                                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
+                                                default:
+                                                }
+                                                return
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        },
+                })
+        } else {
+                w.logger.Info("Unable to watch namespaces since namespace informer is nil")
+        }
+
+        for name, resource := range w.informers {
+                resource.Start(w.stopChannel)
+
+                if ok := w.WaitForNamedCacheSync(name, resource.HasSynced); !ok {
+                        w.logger.Info("skipping informer", "informer", name)
+                        continue
+                }
+
+                // only send an event notification if there isn't one already
+                resource.AddEventHandler(cache.ResourceEventHandlerFuncs{
+                        // these functions only write to the notification channel if it's empty to avoid blocking
+                        // if scrape config updates are being rate-limited
+                        AddFunc: func(obj interface{}) {
+                                select {
+                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
+                                default:
+                                }
+                        },
+                        UpdateFunc: func(oldObj, newObj interface{}) {
+                                select {
+                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
+                                default:
+                                }
+                        },
+                        DeleteFunc: func(obj interface{}) {
+                                select {
+                                case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
+                                default:
+                                }
+                        },
+                })
+        }
+        if !success {
+                return fmt.Errorf("failed to sync one of the caches")
+        }
+
+        // limit the rate of outgoing events
+        w.rateLimitedEventSender(upstreamEvents, notifyEvents)
+
+        <-w.stopChannel
+        return nil
 }
 
 // rateLimitedEventSender sends events to the upstreamEvents channel whenever it gets a notification on the notifyEvents channel,
 // but not more frequently than once per w.eventPeriod.
 func (w *PrometheusCRWatcher) rateLimitedEventSender(upstreamEvents chan Event, notifyEvents chan struct{}) {
-	ticker := time.NewTicker(w.eventInterval)
-	defer ticker.Stop()
-
-	event := Event{
-		Source:  EventSourcePrometheusCR,
-		Watcher: Watcher(w),
-	}
-
-	for {
-		select {
-		case <-w.stopChannel:
-			return
-		case <-ticker.C: // throttle events to avoid excessive updates
-			select {
-			case <-notifyEvents:
-				select {
-				case upstreamEvents <- event:
-				default: // put the notification back in the queue if we can't send it upstream
-					select {
-					case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
-					default:
-					}
-				}
-			default:
-			}
-		}
-	}
+        ticker := time.NewTicker(w.eventInterval)
+        defer ticker.Stop()
+
+        event := Event{
+                Source:  EventSourcePrometheusCR,
+                Watcher: Watcher(w),
+        }
+
+        for {
+                select {
+                case <-w.stopChannel:
+                        return
+                case <-ticker.C: // throttle events to avoid excessive updates
+                        select {
+                        case <-notifyEvents:
+                                select {
+                                case upstreamEvents <- event:
+                                default: // put the notification back in the queue if we can't send it upstream
+                                        select {
+                                        case notifyEvents <- struct{}{}:
+                                        default:
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        default:
+                        }
+                }
+        }
 }

+                        return false
+                }
+        }, time.Second*5, eventInterval/10)
+        _, err = w.kubeMonitoringClient.MonitoringV1().ServiceMonitors("test").Update(context.Background(), serviceMonitor, metav1.UpdateOptions{})
+        require.NoError(t, err)
+        require.Eventually(t, func() bool {
+                select {
+                case <-events:
+                        return true
+                default:
+                        return false
+                }
+        }, time.Second*5, eventInterval/10)
+        elapsedTime := time.Since(startTime)
+        assert.Less(t, eventInterval, elapsedTime)
 }

+++ b/reproduce_issue.go
@@ -0,0 +1,72 @@
+
+package main
+
+import (
+"context"
+"fmt"
+"log"
+"os"
+
+monitoringclient "github.com/prometheus-operator/prometheus-operator/pkg/client/versioned/fake"
+"k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes/fake"
+metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+"github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/cmd/otel-allocator/internal/watcher"
+allocatorconfig "github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-operator/cmd/otel-allocator/internal/config"
+"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+discovery "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/version"
+)
+
+type fakeDiscovery struct {
+*fake.Clientset
+}
+
+func (f *fakeDiscovery) Discovery() *fake.Clientset {
+return f.Clientset
+}
+
+func main() {
+ctx := context.Background()
+
+// Create a fake kubernetes client
+k8sClient := fake.NewSimpleClientset()
+// Set the server version for the discovery client
+k8sClient.Fake.Resources = []*metav1.APIResourceList{
+{
+GroupVersion: "v1",
+APIResources: []metav1.APIResource{
+{Name: "namespaces", Namespaced: false, Kind: "Namespace"},
+},
+},
+}
+
+// The problem is that informers for ServiceMonitor, PodMonitor, Probe, ScrapeConfig 
+// will be created even if they are not enabled in the config or don't exist in the cluster.
+
+// We want to simulate the case where some CRDs are missing.
+// Unfortunately, the fake monitoring client doesn't seem to support missing CRDs easily
+// in the way that it returns an error when creating an informer.
+
+// However, we can still test our changes by checking if informers are created
+// for only the resources we expect.
+
+cfg := allocatorconfig.Config{
+CollectorNamespace: "default",
+PrometheusCR: allocatorconfig.PrometheusCRConfig{
+Enabled:             true,
+PodMonitorSelector: &metav1.LabelSelector{},
+// ServiceMonitorSelector: nil, // Disabled
+},
+}
+
+mClient := monitoringclient.NewSimpleClientset()
+
+w, err := watcher.NewPrometheusCRWatcher(ctx, nil, k8sClient, mClient, cfg)
+if err != nil {
+log.Fatalf("Failed to create watcher: %v", err)
+}
+
+fmt.Printf("Number of informers created: %d\n", len(w.Informers()))
+for name := range w.Informers() {
+fmt.Printf("Informer created for: %s\n", name)
+}
+}
